[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA security issue of type Server-Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m was detected during [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzing. The Jazzer fuzzer raised a `FuzzerSecurityIssueMedium` exception when [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntrusted input triggered an outbound HTTPS connection to jazzer.com:[0m[1;36m443[0m[39m. The [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfailure occurred in Apache Tika’s CSV parser while processing a URL cell, invoking [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJava’s `HttpURLConnection` API.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The fuzzer observed that processing a CSV cell via Apache Tika’s [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TextAndCSVParser` resulted in an unexpected external network connection. Jazzer’s [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSSRF sanitizer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ServerSideRequestForgery.checkSsrf`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m blocked the attempt and threw[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma `FuzzerSecurityIssueMedium` exception, indicating that untrusted data controlled [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe destination of an outbound request.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  Server-Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Untrusted input is used to form network [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrequests, potentially allowing an attacker to probe or exfiltrate internal [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresources.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The exception originates in `ServerSideRequestForgery.checkSsrf`, which detects[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdisallowed socket connections.  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The call chain traverses Java’s socket and HTTPS client classes [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`Socket.connect`, `SSLSocketImpl.connect`, `HttpsClient`, [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`AbstractDelegateHttpsURLConnection.connect`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m before reaching Tika’s CSV parser.  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • In Tika, `TextAndCSVParser.processURL` is invoked from [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TextAndCSVParser.processCell`, which is called by `TextAndCSVParser.parse`.  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The user-written harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`TextAndCSVParserFuzzer.parseOne` → [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m supplies input to Tika, but does not itself initiate network [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minteractions.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The SSRF sanitizer triggered on an attempted connection to `jazzer.com:[0m[1;36m443[0m[39m`, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrevealing that parser logic treats certain CSV fields as URLs and follows them.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code Areas for Investigation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. `org.apache.tika.parser.csv.TextAndCSVParser` – especially `processURL`, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`processCell`, and `parse` methods to understand how URLs are detected and fetched.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Java networking call sites – the usage of [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`HttpURLConnection`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`HttpsURLConnection` within Tika to determine how URL content [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis loaded.  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. SSRF sanitizer integration – [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.ServerSideRequestForgery` methods [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`checkSsrf`, `checkSsrfSocket`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to see the exact conditions under which [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconnections are flagged.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`TextAndCSVParserFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m – while not the root cause, [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreviewing how input is fed may help in reproducing and profiling the behavior.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtika-parsers/tika-parsers-standard/tika-parsers-standard-modules/tika-parser-text-m[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m29[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mDELIMITER_TO_NAME_MAP.put[0m[1;39m([0m[32m','[0m[39m, [0m[32m"comma"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Extending TextAndCSVConfig[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add a new boolean flag `fetchRemoteResources` to control whether the parser [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould perform network fetches for hyperlinks in CSV cells.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Default value: **false** [0m[1;39m([0m[39msecure-by-default; no SSRF risk unless explicitly [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39menabled[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Provide a public getter `[0m[1;35misFetchRemoteResources[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and setter [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35msetFetchRemoteResources[0m[1;39m([0m[39mboolean[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` so clients can enable the feature via [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ParseContext`.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Example additions in TextAndCSVConfig.java:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     private boolean fetchRemoteResources = false;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[35m/[0m[39m** [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      * Whether to fetch and parse remote resources referenced by =HYPERLINK [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mformulas.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      * Default is false to prevent SSRF.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     public boolean [0m[1;35misFetchRemoteResources[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         return fetchRemoteResources;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     public void [0m[1;35msetFetchRemoteResources[0m[1;39m([0m[39mboolean fetchRemoteResources[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         this.fetchRemoteResources = fetchRemoteResources;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This change preserves all existing functionality when clients do not override [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe default [0m[1;39m([0m[39mremote fetching remains off unless opted in[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Guarding processURL Invocation in TextAndCSVParser[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `[0m[1;35mprocessCell[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString cellContent, XHTMLContentHandler xhtml, Metadata [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmetadata, ParseContext context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, retrieve the `TextAndCSVConfig` from the [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ParseContext` [0m[1;39m([0m[39musing the existing `defaultTextAndCSVConfig`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and only invoke [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` if `[0m[1;35mconfig.isFetchRemoteResources[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` returns true.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Also still emit the `<a [0m[33mhref[0m[39m=[0m[32m"..."[0m[39m>[0m[33m...[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95ma[0m[39m>` anchor unconditionally [0m[1;39m([0m[39mso [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdownstream consumers see the hyperlink text[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, but skip the network fetch when [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdisabled.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Example patch outline in TextAndCSVParser.java:[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     private void [0m[1;35mprocessCell[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString cellContent, XHTMLContentHandler xhtml,[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                              Metadata metadata,[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                              ParseContext context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException, [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSAXException [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mxhtml.startElement[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTD[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         Matcher m = [0m[1;35mHYPERLINK_PATTERN.matcher[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcellContent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mm.find[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             String url = [0m[1;35mm.group[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             String name = [0m[1;35mm.group[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mStringUtils.isBlank[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 name = url;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Always emit the <a> element[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;35mxhtml.startElement[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"a"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"href"[0m[39m, url[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;35mxhtml.characters[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;35mxhtml.endElement[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"a"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Conditionally fetch remote resource[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             TextAndCSVConfig config = [0m[1;35mcontext.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTextAndCSVConfig.class, [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefaultTextAndCSVConfig[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mconfig.isFetchRemoteResources[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 [0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[39murl, name, xhtml, metadata, context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;35mxhtml.characters[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcellContent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mxhtml.endElement[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTD[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No other changes to `processURL` are required; it remains responsible for [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing embedded content when authorized.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Documentation and Tests[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Update the Tika CSV parser documentation to mention the new [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`fetchRemoteResources` flag and its default setting.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add a unit test in the standard Tika test suite to verify:[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • By default, hyperlinks are not fetched [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno network activity; parser output [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mincludes `<a>` but no embedded resource metadata[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • When `fetchRemoteResources` is enabled via `ParseContext`, the parser [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfetches and embeds content as before.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRationale:[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Introducing a config guard isolates the SSRF control to one feature flag without [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maltering other CSV parsing behaviors.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Defaulting `fetchRemoteResources` to `false` preserves backward compatibility in [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe sense of no network actions for existing users, and provides secure defaults.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Only minimal changes in two classes [0m[1;39m([0m[39mTextAndCSVConfig and TextAndCSVParser[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensure existing parsing logic and performance are unaffected unless remote fetches [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mare explicitly requested.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No modifications are made to the harness, fuzzing logic, utility functions, or [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal libraries—only core parser code is patched.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This approach aligns with other Tika parsers that guard expensive or risky [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperations behind parser-specific configs [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., disabling external DTD fetching in[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mXML parsers[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPotential Side Effects and Mitigations:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Clients who rely on automatic hyperlink fetching will notice the behavior change;[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe documentation and release notes should clearly describe the new default.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- In performance-sensitive environments, fetching remains off by default, avoiding [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munintended delays.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No additional exception paths are introduced; if `fetchRemoteResources` is [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39menabled, `processURL` still catches downstream exceptions and records them in [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmetadata, maintaining existing resilience.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m262[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m263[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35mxhtml.characters[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcellContent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. TextAndCSVConfig.java – Correct placement of `fetchRemoteResources`:[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Add the new `fetchRemoteResources` field and its accessor methods *inside* [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe class body—*after* the existing delimiter‐map getters/setters but *before* the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclosing `[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` of the class. Do **not** insert them between or inside static [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minitializer blocks.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Annotate the field [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand setter[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with Tika’s `@Field` annotation so that it [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcan be configured via the parser’s `ParseContext`:[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      import org.apache.tika.config.Field;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      …[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      public class TextAndCSVConfig implements Serializable [0m[1;39m{[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m existing static blocks, maps, getters/setters[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[39m**[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           * Whether to fetch and parse remote resources referenced by =HYPERLINK [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mformulas.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           * Default is false to prevent SSRF.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          @Field[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          private boolean fetchRemoteResources = false;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          public boolean [0m[1;35misFetchRemoteResources[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              return fetchRemoteResources;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          @Field[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          public void [0m[1;35msetFetchRemoteResources[0m[1;39m([0m[39mboolean fetchRemoteResources[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              this.fetchRemoteResources = fetchRemoteResources;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Ensure there is a single closing brace `[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` for the class at the end [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m~[0m[1;36m58[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Remove any stray/mismatched braces that were introduced by the previous [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpatch.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. TextAndCSVParser.java – Guard remote fetch behind the flag:[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. At the top of the file, verify you have:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      import org.apache.tika.parser.csv.TextAndCSVConfig;[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Ensure there’s a `defaultTextAndCSVConfig` instance available, for example:[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      private static final TextAndCSVConfig defaultTextAndCSVConfig = new [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mTextAndCSVConfig[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIf it doesn’t exist, declare it once near other static defaults.[0m[1;39m)[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. In `[0m[1;35mprocessCell[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m261[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, replace the unconditional [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` call with:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      TextAndCSVConfig config = [0m[1;35mcontext.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTextAndCSVConfig.class, [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefaultTextAndCSVConfig[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mconfig.isFetchRemoteResources[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[39murl, name, xhtml, metadata, context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      This preserves the existing XHTML output but only follows hyperlinks when the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mflag is enabled.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Imports and configuration wiring:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add `import org.apache.tika.config.Field;` to `TextAndCSVConfig.java`.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add or confirm `import org.apache.tika.parser.csv.TextAndCSVConfig;` in [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TextAndCSVParser.java`.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Do **not** modify any harness/fuzzing code or external libraries.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Placing the field and methods after the existing getters/setters ensures they [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mare within the class’s braces and outside static blocks, resolving the “illegal [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstart of type” and related compiler errors.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Annotating with `@Field` integrates with Tika’s `ParseContext` so users can [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39menable remote fetch via standard configuration [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., in a `tika-config.xml` or [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprogrammatic context injection[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Guarding `[0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` preserves existing link rendering while preventing [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSSRF by default; it only fetches remote content if explicitly requested.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No other functionality is removed or altered—delimiter mapping and other [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing logic remain intact, and all existing tests should continue passing.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Side Effects & Mitigation:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By default, no remote connections will be attempted, which is the safest [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Users who rely on hyperlink previews or inline resource fetching will need to [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mset `[0m[33mfetchRemoteResources[0m[39m=[0m[35mtrue[0m[39m` in their `ParseContext`.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Review any documentation or examples to mention the new flag.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mOnce these changes are applied, the project should compile cleanly, and SSRF alerts[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwill be suppressed unless remote fetching is explicitly enabled. [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
